# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-loki`, `github.com/sg-evals/grafana-mimir`

# Grafana Alerting Rule Evaluation to Notification Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a Grafana unified alerting rule is evaluated and fired in grafana/grafana. Find Go source files implementing: the rule scheduler, the rule evaluation, the alert state transition, and the alert notification dispatch to receivers.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

It can happen,\n305: \t\t\t\t\t// if we have an alert with state and we do file provision with stateful Grafana, that state\n306: \t\t\t\t\t// lingers in DB and won't be cleaned up until next alert rule update.\n307: \t\t\t\t\tneedReset = needReset || (currentFingerprint == 0 && isPaused)\n308: \t\t\t\t\tif needReset {\n309: \t\t\t\t\t\ta.resetState(grafanaCtx, ctx.rule, isPaused)\n310: Notification Chain\\n\\n### Overview\\nGrafana's unified alerting system follows a pipeline architecture that moves alert rules from scheduling through evaluation, state management, and finally to notification dispatch.\\n\\n### 1. Rule Scheduler (Scheduling Layer)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`**\\n\\nThe scheduler is the entry point for the entire alerting pipeline:\\n- `schedule.Run()`: Main event loop that processes scheduler ticks at regular intervals (baseInterval)\\n- `schedule.processTick()`: Called on each tick to determine which rules should be evaluated\\n  - Updates schedulable alert rules from the database\\n  - Determines which rules are ready to run based on their evaluation intervals\\n  - Dispatches ready rules to their evaluation routines using `sequence` and `runJobFn`\\n  - `runJobFn()`: Wrapper function that calls `alertRule.Eval()` with the evaluation parameters\\n\\nThe scheduler maintains:\\n- A registry of active alert rules (`ruleRegistry`)\\n- Metrics for scheduler performance\\n- Configuration including base interval, retry settings, and external URL\\n- Reference to the state manager and alertsSender (AlertsRouter)\\n\\n### 2. Alert Rule Execution (Rule Evaluation Routine)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`**\\n\\nEach alert rule runs in its own goroutine managed by the `alertRule` struct:\\n- `alertRule.Run()`: Main loop for the rule's evaluation routine\\n  - Receives evaluation signals on `evalCh` channel\\n  - Processes rule updates on `updateCh` channel\\n  - Manages rule state and fingerprints to detect changes\\n  - On evaluation signal, calls `evaluate()`\\n  \\n- `alertRule.Eval()`: Called by scheduler to send evaluation signal\\n  - Queues the evaluation for the rule routine to process\\n  - Handles dropped evaluations if rule is busy\\n  \\n- `alertRule.evaluate()`: Performs the actual rule evaluation\\n  - Creates evaluation context with user and loaded metrics\\n  - Calls `evalFactory.Create()` to build the evaluator pipeline\\n  - Calls evaluator's `Evaluate()` to execute queries and condition\\n  - Handles retries with exponential backoff on failure\\n  - On success, calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` with:\\n    - Evaluation results\\n    - Extra labels (folder title, custom labels)\\n    - Sender callback function\\n  - Observes evaluation duration metrics\\n\\n### 3. Rule Condition Evaluation\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`**\\n\\nThe evaluation engine executes the alert rule's query and condition:\\n- `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()`: Main evaluation method\\n  - Calls `EvaluateRaw()` to execute the query pipeline\\n  - Converts backend response to alert states using `EvaluateAlert()`\\n  \\n- `EvaluateRaw()`: Executes the expression pipeline\\n  - Creates context with timeout\\n  - Calls expression service to execute datasource queries and expressions\\n  - Validates result size against evaluation limits\\n  - Returns raw backend response\\n\\n- `EvaluateAlert()`: Converts query results to alert states\\n  - Processes each result to determine alert state (Alerting, Normal, NoData, etc.)\\n  - Creates Result objects with:\\n    - Instance labels (from datasource results)\\n    - State (Alerting, Normal, Pending, etc.)\\n    - Evaluation time and duration\\n    - Values from instant vectors or reduce expressions\\n\\n### 4. Alert State Transition and Management\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` and `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`**\\n\\nAlert states track the condition and history of each alert instance:\\n- `State` struct: Represents a single alert instance state\\n  - Current state (Alerting, Normal, Pending, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n  - StateReason: Human-readable reason for state\\n  - Labels and Annotations: From rule configuration and evaluation results\\n  - StartsAt/EndsAt: Timestamps for state periods\\n  - FiredAt: When state first transitioned to Alerting\\n  - ResolvedAt: When state transitioned back to Normal\\n  - LastSentAt: When alert was last sent to alertmanager\\n\\n- `Manager.ProcessEvalResults()`: Main state processing function\\n  - Called by alert rule after evaluation with results\\n  - Takes evaluation results and updates alert instance states\\n  - `setNextStateForRule()`: Determines new state for each alert instance\\n    - Gets current state from cache\\n    - Calls `state.transition()` to calculate new state based on:\\n      - Previous state\\n      - Current evaluation result\\n      - Rule configuration (NoDataState, ExecErrState)\\n      - Duration thresholds (for Pending \u2192 Alerting transitions)\\n    - Updates state in cache\\n  - `processMissingSeriesStates()`: Handles series that were in previous eval but not current\\n    - Transitions these to Recovering state\\n  - `updateLastSentAt()`: Determines which state transitions need to be sent\\n    - Uses ResendDelay (30 seconds) to avoid redundant notifications\\n    - Uses ResolvedRetention to keep resolved alerts briefly\\n  - Persists states to instanceStore and historian\\n  - Invokes sender callback with StateTransitions to send\\n\\n- `StateTransition`: Represents a state change\\n  - Current State with all details\\n  - PreviousState: For comparison\\n  - PreviousStateReason: For context\\n\\n### 5. Alert Notification Dispatch\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`**\\n\\nAlert rule sends state transitions to notification system:\\n- `alertRule.send()`: Converts state transitions to PostableAlerts\\n  - Converts each StateTransition to PostableAlert format\\n  - Calls `alertsSender.Send()` (which is AlertsRouter)\\n  - Logs alert sending with transition count\\n\\n### 6. Alerts Router (AlertsSender Implementation)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`**\\n\\nThe AlertsRouter decides where alerts should be sent:\\n- `AlertsRouter.Send()`: Routes alerts to internal and/or external alertmanagers\\n  - Receives: orgID, rule key, PostableAlerts\\n  - Checks configuration for SendAlertsTo choice:\\n    - InternalAlertmanager: Send to internal Grafana alertmanager\\n    - ExternalAlertmanagers: Send to external Prometheus Alertmanagers\\n    - Both: Send to both (default fallback)\\n  - For internal alertmanager:\\n    - Gets MultiOrgAlertmanager for organization\\n    - Calls `PutAlerts()` to submit alerts\\n  - For external alertmanagers:\\n    - Gets ExternalAlertmanager sender for organization\\n    - Calls `SendAlerts()` to dispatch alerts\\n  - Handles missing alertmanagers gracefully\\n\\n### 7. Internal Alertmanager (Notification Management)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`**\\n\\nManages per-organization Alertmanager instances:\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()`: Gets alertmanager for organization\\n  - Creates new alertmanager if not exists\\n  - Returns Alertmanager interface with PutAlerts() method\\n  - Alertmanager processes alerts through:\\n    - Silencing rules\\n    - Notification routing\\n    - Grouping (alert_grouping_config)\\n    - Receiver notifications\\n\\n- `Alertmanager.PutAlerts()`: Submits alerts to alertmanager\\n  - Uses internal alerting library (grafana/alerting)\\n  - Processes through notification pipeline\\n  - Sends to configured receivers\\n  - Records notification history\\n\\n### 8. External Alertmanager Dispatch\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go`**\\n\\nHandles sending alerts to external Prometheus Alertmanagers:\\n- `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`: Queues alerts for delivery\\n  - Converts PostableAlerts to Alert format\\n  - Sanitizes label names for Prometheus compatibility\\n  - Queues alerts in Manager's queue\\n  - Notifies sendLoop to process queue\\n\\n- `Manager.Send()`: Queues alerts\\n  - Applies relabel configs and external labels\\n  - Manages queue capacity\\n  - Signals sendLoop to process\\n\\n- `Manager.sendLoop()`: Batch dispatcher\\n  - Waits for queue signal\\n  - Takes next batch (up to MaxBatchSize)\\n  - Calls `sendAll()` to post to Alertmanagers\\n  - Handles retries and errors\\n  - Posts to `/api/v2/alerts` endpoint on each Alertmanager\\n\\n- `Manager.targetUpdateLoop()`: Discovers Alertmanager endpoints\\n  - Receives target updates from service discovery\\n  - Syncs active Alertmanager list\\n  - Manages alertmanagerSet for each configuration\\n\\n### Complete Evaluation Flow\\n\\n1. **Scheduling** \u2192 `schedule.Run()` \u2192 `processTick()` \u2192 identifies rules ready to evaluate\\n2. **Dispatch** \u2192 `runJobFn()` \u2192 `alertRule.Eval()` signals rule routine\\n3. **Evaluation** \u2192 `alertRule.Run()` receives signal \u2192 `evaluate()` executes\\n4. **Query Execution** \u2192 `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` \u2192 expression pipeline\\n5. **State Calculation** \u2192 `state.Manager.ProcessEvalResults()` \u2192 state transitions\\n6. **State Determination** \u2192 `setNextStateForRule()` \u2192 new alert states\\n7. **Notification Decision** \u2192 `updateLastSentAt()` \u2192 which states to send\\n8. **Alert Sending** \u2192 `alertRule.send()` \u2192 `AlertsRouter.Send()`\\n9. **Internal Route** \u2192 `MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts()` \u2192 internal alertmanager\\n10. **External Route** \u2192 `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()` \u2192 `Manager.sendLoop()` \u2192 HTTP POST\\n11. **Receiver Dispatch** \u2192 Alertmanager routes to configured receivers\\n\\nThis architecture separates concerns cleanly: scheduling determines timing, evaluation executes queries, state management tracks instances, and notification routing delivers alerts to appropriate destinations.\"\n}\n",

Notification Chain\\n\\n### Overview\\nGrafana's unified alerting system follows a pipeline architecture that moves alert rules from scheduling through evaluation, state management, and finally to notification dispatch.\\n\\n### 1. Rule Scheduler (Scheduling Layer)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/schedule.go`**\\n\\nThe scheduler is the entry point for the entire alerting pipeline:\\n- `schedule.Run()`: Main event loop that processes scheduler ticks at regular intervals (baseInterval)\\n- `schedule.processTick()`: Called on each tick to determine which rules should be evaluated\\n  - Updates schedulable alert rules from the database\\n  - Determines which rules are ready to run based on their evaluation intervals\\n  - Dispatches ready rules to their evaluation routines using `sequence` and `runJobFn`\\n  - `runJobFn()`: Wrapper function that calls `alertRule.Eval()` with the evaluation parameters\\n\\nThe scheduler maintains:\\n- A registry of active alert rules (`ruleRegistry`)\\n- Metrics for scheduler performance\\n- Configuration including base interval, retry settings, and external URL\\n- Reference to the state manager and alertsSender (AlertsRouter)\\n\\n### 2. Alert Rule Execution (Rule Evaluation Routine)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`**\\n\\nEach alert rule runs in its own goroutine managed by the `alertRule` struct:\\n- `alertRule.Run()`: Main loop for the rule's evaluation routine\\n  - Receives evaluation signals on `evalCh` channel\\n  - Processes rule updates on `updateCh` channel\\n  - Manages rule state and fingerprints to detect changes\\n  - On evaluation signal, calls `evaluate()`\\n  \\n- `alertRule.Eval()`: Called by scheduler to send evaluation signal\\n  - Queues the evaluation for the rule routine to process\\n  - Handles dropped evaluations if rule is busy\\n  \\n- `alertRule.evaluate()`: Performs the actual rule evaluation\\n  - Creates evaluation context with user and loaded metrics\\n  - Calls `evalFactory.Create()` to build the evaluator pipeline\\n  - Calls evaluator's `Evaluate()` to execute queries and condition\\n  - Handles retries with exponential backoff on failure\\n  - On success, calls `stateManager.ProcessEvalResults()` with:\\n    - Evaluation results\\n    - Extra labels (folder title, custom labels)\\n    - Sender callback function\\n  - Observes evaluation duration metrics\\n\\n### 3. Rule Condition Evaluation\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/eval/eval.go`**\\n\\nThe evaluation engine executes the alert rule's query and condition:\\n- `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()`: Main evaluation method\\n  - Calls `EvaluateRaw()` to execute the query pipeline\\n  - Converts backend response to alert states using `EvaluateAlert()`\\n  \\n- `EvaluateRaw()`: Executes the expression pipeline\\n  - Creates context with timeout\\n  - Calls expression service to execute datasource queries and expressions\\n  - Validates result size against evaluation limits\\n  - Returns raw backend response\\n\\n- `EvaluateAlert()`: Converts query results to alert states\\n  - Processes each result to determine alert state (Alerting, Normal, NoData, etc.)\\n  - Creates Result objects with:\\n    - Instance labels (from datasource results)\\n    - State (Alerting, Normal, Pending, etc.)\\n    - Evaluation time and duration\\n    - Values from instant vectors or reduce expressions\\n\\n### 4. Alert State Transition and Management\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/state/state.go` and `pkg/services/ngalert/state/manager.go`**\\n\\nAlert states track the condition and history of each alert instance:\\n- `State` struct: Represents a single alert instance state\\n  - Current state (Alerting, Normal, Pending, NoData, Error, Recovering)\\n  - StateReason: Human-readable reason for state\\n  - Labels and Annotations: From rule configuration and evaluation results\\n  - StartsAt/EndsAt: Timestamps for state periods\\n  - FiredAt: When state first transitioned to Alerting\\n  - ResolvedAt: When state transitioned back to Normal\\n  - LastSentAt: When alert was last sent to alertmanager\\n\\n- `Manager.ProcessEvalResults()`: Main state processing function\\n  - Called by alert rule after evaluation with results\\n  - Takes evaluation results and updates alert instance states\\n  - `setNextStateForRule()`: Determines new state for each alert instance\\n    - Gets current state from cache\\n    - Calls `state.transition()` to calculate new state based on:\\n      - Previous state\\n      - Current evaluation result\\n      - Rule configuration (NoDataState, ExecErrState)\\n      - Duration thresholds (for Pending \u2192 Alerting transitions)\\n    - Updates state in cache\\n  - `processMissingSeriesStates()`: Handles series that were in previous eval but not current\\n    - Transitions these to Recovering state\\n  - `updateLastSentAt()`: Determines which state transitions need to be sent\\n    - Uses ResendDelay (30 seconds) to avoid redundant notifications\\n    - Uses ResolvedRetention to keep resolved alerts briefly\\n  - Persists states to instanceStore and historian\\n  - Invokes sender callback with StateTransitions to send\\n\\n- `StateTransition`: Represents a state change\\n  - Current State with all details\\n  - PreviousState: For comparison\\n  - PreviousStateReason: For context\\n\\n### 5. Alert Notification Dispatch\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/alert_rule.go`**\\n\\nAlert rule sends state transitions to notification system:\\n- `alertRule.send()`: Converts state transitions to PostableAlerts\\n  - Converts each StateTransition to PostableAlert format\\n  - Calls `alertsSender.Send()` (which is AlertsRouter)\\n  - Logs alert sending with transition count\\n\\n### 6. Alerts Router (AlertsSender Implementation)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/router.go`**\\n\\nThe AlertsRouter decides where alerts should be sent:\\n- `AlertsRouter.Send()`: Routes alerts to internal and/or external alertmanagers\\n  - Receives: orgID, rule key, PostableAlerts\\n  - Checks configuration for SendAlertsTo choice:\\n    - InternalAlertmanager: Send to internal Grafana alertmanager\\n    - ExternalAlertmanagers: Send to external Prometheus Alertmanagers\\n    - Both: Send to both (default fallback)\\n  - For internal alertmanager:\\n    - Gets MultiOrgAlertmanager for organization\\n    - Calls `PutAlerts()` to submit alerts\\n  - For external alertmanagers:\\n    - Gets ExternalAlertmanager sender for organization\\n    - Calls `SendAlerts()` to dispatch alerts\\n  - Handles missing alertmanagers gracefully\\n\\n### 7. Internal Alertmanager (Notification Management)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`**\\n\\nManages per-organization Alertmanager instances:\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()`: Gets alertmanager for organization\\n  - Creates new alertmanager if not exists\\n  - Returns Alertmanager interface with PutAlerts() method\\n  - Alertmanager processes alerts through:\\n    - Silencing rules\\n    - Notification routing\\n    - Grouping (alert_grouping_config)\\n    - Receiver notifications\\n\\n- `Alertmanager.PutAlerts()`: Submits alerts to alertmanager\\n  - Uses internal alerting library (grafana/alerting)\\n  - Processes through notification pipeline\\n  - Sends to configured receivers\\n  - Records notification history\\n\\n### 8. External Alertmanager Dispatch\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go`**\\n\\nHandles sending alerts to external Prometheus Alertmanagers:\\n- `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`: Queues alerts for delivery\\n  - Converts PostableAlerts to Alert format\\n  - Sanitizes label names for Prometheus compatibility\\n  - Queues alerts in Manager's queue\\n  - Notifies sendLoop to process queue\\n\\n- `Manager.Send()`: Queues alerts\\n  - Applies relabel configs and external labels\\n  - Manages queue capacity\\n  - Signals sendLoop to process\\n\\n- `Manager.sendLoop()`: Batch dispatcher\\n  - Waits for queue signal\\n  - Takes next batch (up to MaxBatchSize)\\n  - Calls `sendAll()` to post to Alertmanagers\\n  - Handles retries and errors\\n  - Posts to `/api/v2/alerts` endpoint on each Alertmanager\\n\\n- `Manager.targetUpdateLoop()`: Discovers Alertmanager endpoints\\n  - Receives target updates from service discovery\\n  - Syncs active Alertmanager list\\n  - Manages alertmanagerSet for each configuration\\n\\n### Complete Evaluation Flow\\n\\n1. **Scheduling** \u2192 `schedule.Run()` \u2192 `processTick()` \u2192 identifies rules ready to evaluate\\n2. **Dispatch** \u2192 `runJobFn()` \u2192 `alertRule.Eval()` signals rule routine\\n3. **Evaluation** \u2192 `alertRule.Run()` receives signal \u2192 `evaluate()` executes\\n4. **Query Execution** \u2192 `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` \u2192 expression pipeline\\n5. **State Calculation** \u2192 `state.Manager.ProcessEvalResults()` \u2192 state transitions\\n6. **State Determination** \u2192 `setNextStateForRule()` \u2192 new alert states\\n7. **Notification Decision** \u2192 `updateLastSentAt()` \u2192 which states to send\\n8. **Alert Sending** \u2192 `alertRule.send()` \u2192 `AlertsRouter.Send()`\\n9. **Internal Route** \u2192 `MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts()` \u2192 internal alertmanager\\n10. **External Route** \u2192 `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()` \u2192 `Manager.sendLoop()` \u2192 HTTP POST\\n11. **Receiver Dispatch** \u2192 Alertmanager routes to configured receivers\\n\\nThis architecture separates concerns cleanly: scheduling determines timing, evaluation executes queries, state management tracks instances, and notification routing delivers alerts to appropriate destinations.\"\n}\n",

Internal Alertmanager (Notification Management)\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/multiorg_alertmanager.go`**\\n\\nManages per-organization Alertmanager instances:\\n- `MultiOrgAlertmanager.AlertmanagerFor()`: Gets alertmanager for organization\\n  - Creates new alertmanager if not exists\\n  - Returns Alertmanager interface with PutAlerts() method\\n  - Alertmanager processes alerts through:\\n    - Silencing rules\\n    - Notification routing\\n    - Grouping (alert_grouping_config)\\n    - Receiver notifications\\n\\n- `Alertmanager.PutAlerts()`: Submits alerts to alertmanager\\n  - Uses internal alerting library (grafana/alerting)\\n  - Processes through notification pipeline\\n  - Sends to configured receivers\\n  - Records notification history\\n\\n### 8. External Alertmanager Dispatch\\n\\n**File: `pkg/services/ngalert/sender/sender.go`**\\n\\nHandles sending alerts to external Prometheus Alertmanagers:\\n- `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()`: Queues alerts for delivery\\n  - Converts PostableAlerts to Alert format\\n  - Sanitizes label names for Prometheus compatibility\\n  - Queues alerts in Manager's queue\\n  - Notifies sendLoop to process queue\\n\\n- `Manager.Send()`: Queues alerts\\n  - Applies relabel configs and external labels\\n  - Manages queue capacity\\n  - Signals sendLoop to process\\n\\n- `Manager.sendLoop()`: Batch dispatcher\\n  - Waits for queue signal\\n  - Takes next batch (up to MaxBatchSize)\\n  - Calls `sendAll()` to post to Alertmanagers\\n  - Handles retries and errors\\n  - Posts to `/api/v2/alerts` endpoint on each Alertmanager\\n\\n- `Manager.targetUpdateLoop()`: Discovers Alertmanager endpoints\\n  - Receives target updates from service discovery\\n  - Syncs active Alertmanager list\\n  - Manages alertmanagerSet for each configuration\\n\\n### Complete Evaluation Flow\\n\\n1. **Scheduling** \u2192 `schedule.Run()` \u2192 `processTick()` \u2192 identifies rules ready to evaluate\\n2. **Dispatch** \u2192 `runJobFn()` \u2192 `alertRule.Eval()` signals rule routine\\n3. **Evaluation** \u2192 `alertRule.Run()` receives signal \u2192 `evaluate()` executes\\n4. **Query Execution** \u2192 `conditionEvaluator.Evaluate()` \u2192 expression pipeline\\n5. **State Calculation** \u2192 `state.Manager.ProcessEvalResults()` \u2192 state transitions\\n6. **State Determination** \u2192 `setNextStateForRule()` \u2192 new alert states\\n7. **Notification Decision** \u2192 `updateLastSentAt()` \u2192 which states to send\\n8. **Alert Sending** \u2192 `alertRule.send()` \u2192 `AlertsRouter.Send()`\\n9. **Internal Route** \u2192 `MultiOrgAlertmanager.PutAlerts()` \u2192 internal alertmanager\\n10. **External Route** \u2192 `ExternalAlertmanager.SendAlerts()` \u2192 `Manager.sendLoop()` \u2192 HTTP POST\\n11. **Receiver Dispatch** \u2192 Alertmanager routes to configured receivers\\n\\nThis architecture separates concerns cleanly: scheduling determines timing, evaluation executes queries, state management tracks instances, and notification routing delivers alerts to appropriate destinations.\"\n}\n",
